async function resolveLineMasterByLang(paramLineId, selectedLang) {
    const lineMastersData = await getLineMastersByLang(selectedLang);
    const lineMasters = lineMastersData.lst;

    return lineMasters.find(lineMaster =>
        lineMaster.ryokakuSenkuCd === paramLineId
    );
}

const getServerDateTime = () => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();
    $.ajax({
        url: window.location.href,
        type: 'GET',
        cache: false,
        error: defer.reject
    }).done(function (data, status, xhr) {
        const dateStr = xhr.getResponseHeader('Date');
        if (dateStr) {
            defer.resolve(new Date(dateStr));
        } else {
            defer.reject('No Date header');
        }
    });
    return defer.promise();
}

const createHeader = (additionalItem = null) => {
    try {
        window.serverDateReady = (async function () {
            try {
                window.serverDate = await getServerDateTime();
            } catch (e) {
                window.serverDate = new Date();
            }
        })();

        $('header').load('header.html', () => {
            if (paramLang === 'ja') {
                $('.to_jr_tokai_top').attr('href', JR_TOKAI_TOP_URL);
            } else {
                $('.to_jr_tokai_top').addClass('to_jr_tokai_top--en');
                $('.to_jr_tokai_top').attr('href', `${JR_TOKAI_TOP_GLOBAL_URL}${paramLang}/`);
            }

            $('.top').attr('href', `${TOP}?lang=${paramLang}`);
            $('.top .wrapper span').text(getText('header.menus.top'));

            $('.language.header__menu').show();
            $('.language-selection').append($('<option value="">LANGUAGE</option>'));
            Object.keys(languages).forEach(key => {
                $('.language-selection').append($(`<option value="${key}">${languages[key]}</option>`));
            });

            return getText('delay_certificate_list.screen_title');
        case DELAY_CERTIFICATE:
            return getText('delay_certificate.screen_title');
        case DELAY_HIST

const createServiceError = (parent) => {
    if (parent) {
        parent.css('display', 'none');
        parent.load('service_error.html', () => {
            parent.show();
            $('.service-error h4').html(getText('service_error.message'));
            $('.return-top').css('display', 'none');
        });

        return;
    }

    $('.service-error-wrap').load('service_error.html', () => {
        $('.service-error-wrap').show();
        $('.service-error h4').html(getText('service_error.message'));
        $('.return-top').css('display', 'none');
    });
}

                ${getText('delay_certificate_list.screen_title')}
            </a>`;
            return `${breadcrumbList}${delayCertListLink}

const resolveBreadcrumbList = () => {
    const currentScreenName = location.pathname.replace(/\/+$/, '').split('/').pop();

    const jrTokaiTop = paramLang === 'ja' ?
        `<a href="${JR_TOKAI_TOP_URL}">` : `<a href="${JR_TOKAI_TOP_GLOBAL_URL}${paramLang}/">`;
    const topScreenName = getText('breadcrumb_list.top');

    let breadcrumbList = `${jrTokaiTop}${getText('breadcrumb_list.jr_tokai_top')}</a> ${BREADCRUMB_LIST_SEPARATOR} `;
    breadcrumbList = currentScreenName === TOP ? `${breadcrumbList} ${topScreenName}`
        : `${breadcrumbList} <a href="${TOP}?lang=${paramLang}">${topScreenName}</a> ${BREADCRUMB_LIST_SEPARATOR} `;

    switch (currentScreenName) {
        case TOP:
            return breadcrumbList;
        case TRAIN_INFORMATION:
            return `${breadcrumbList}${getText('train_information.screen_title')}`;
        case EXPRESS_INFORMATION:
            return `${breadcrumbList}${getText('express_information.screen_title')}`;
        case STATUS_DETAIL:
            return resolveStatusDetailBreadcrumbList(breadcrumbList);
        case DELAY_CERTIFICATE_LIST:
            return `${breadcrumbList}${getText('delay_certificate_list.screen_title')}`;
        case DELAY_CERTIFICATE:
            return resolveDelayCertificateBreadcrumbList(breadcrumbList);
        case DELAY_HISTORY:
            const delayCertListLink = `<a href="${DELAY_CERTIFICATE_LIST}">
                ${getText('delay_certificate_list.screen_title')}
    

--- candidate ---
dcrumbList);
        case DELAY_HISTORY:
            const delayCertListLink = `<a href="${DELAY_CERTIFICATE_LIST}">
                ${getText('delay_certificate_list.screen_title')}
            </a>`;
            return `${breadcrumbList}${delayCertListLink}
                 ${BREADCRUMB_LIST_SEPARATOR} ${getText('delay_history.screen_title')}`;
        case FAQ:
            return `${breadcrumbList}${getText('faq.screen_title')}`;
        default:
            return '';
    }
}

const resolveScreenTitle = () => {
    const currentScreenName = location.pathname.replace(/\/+$/, '').split('/').pop();

    switch (currentScreenName) {
        case TOP:
            return getText('index.screen_title');
        case TRAIN_INFORMATION:
            return getText('train_information.screen_title');
        case EXPRESS_INFORMATION:
            return getText('express_information.screen_title');
        case STATUS_DETAIL:
            return resolveStatusDetailScreenTitle();
        case DELAY_CERTIFICATE_LIST:
            return getText('delay_certificate_list.screen_title');
        case DELAY_CERTIFICATE:
            return getText('delay_certificate.screen_title');
        case DELAY_HISTORY:
            return getText('delay_history.screen_title');
        case FAQ:
            return getText('faq.screen_title');
        default:
            return '';
    }
}

onst main = document.querySelector("main");

    const observer = new ResizeObserver(() => {
        const height = header.getBoundingClientRect().height;
        if (!scheduled && height !== headerSize) {
            scheduled = true;
            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                headerSize = height;
                main.style.setProperty('--height', `${height}px`);
                scheduled = false;
            });
        }
    });
    observer.observe(header);
}

const backToTop = () => {
    const scrollElement = 'main';
    $(scrollElement).animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 500);
}

const reloadPage = () => {
    
	let scrollPos = document.querySelector('main').scrollTop;
	if(document.querySelector('.tab__content') 
	  && document.querySelector('.tab__content').scrollTop >= 35){
		scrollPos = document.querySelector('.tab__content').scrollTop;
		sessionStorage.setItem('scrollFlg', '0');
	}else{
		sessionStorage.setItem('scrollFlg', '1');
	}
	const pos = parseInt(sessionStorage.getItem('scrollPos'), 10);

	if (!Number.isNaN(pos) && pos > 0) {
	    scrollPos = pos
	}

    sessionStorage.setItem('scrollPos', scrollPos);
    sessionStorage.setItem('doReload', '1');

    window.location.href = window.location.href;
}

const isSp = () => {
    if (matchMedia && matchMedia('(max-device-width: 768px)').matches) {
        return true;
    }

    return false;
}

    if (lineMaster.senkuKbn && (Number(lineMaster.senkuKbn) === 1)) {
        return true;
    }

    return false;
}

const isExpress = (lineMaster) => {
    if (lineMaster.senkuKbn && (Number(lineMaster.senkuKbn) === 3 || Number(lineMaster.senkuKbn) === 4)) {
        return true;
    }

    return false;
}

const isOtherHomeLiner = (lineMaster) => {
    return lineMaster.ryokakuSenkuCd === OTHER_HOME_LINER_LINE_ID;
}

async function resolveLineMasterByLang(paramLineId, selectedLang) {
    const lineMastersData = await getLineMastersByLang(selectedLang);
    const lineMasters = lineMastersData.lst;

    return lineMasters.find(lineMaster =>
        lineMaster.ryokakuSenkuCd === paramLineId
    );
}

const getServerDateTime = () => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();
    $.ajax({
        url: window.location.href,
        type: 'GET',
        cache: false,
        error: defer.reject
    }).done(function (data, status, xhr) {
        const dateStr = xhr.getResponseHeader('Date');
        if (dateStr) {
            defer.resolve(new Date(dateStr));
        } else {
            defer.reject('No Date header');
        }
    });
    return defer.promise();
}

=== function getServiceStatus ===
const getServiceStatus = () => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: `${SERVICE_STATUS_PATH}/hp_service_jotai_kanri.json`,
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        serviceStatus = data;
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getServiceStatus';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}


=== function getLineMasters ===
const getLineMasters = () => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: `${LINE_MASTER_PATH}/hp_senku_master_${paramLang}.json`,
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        lineMasters = data.lst;
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getLineMasters';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}


=== function getOperationStatus ===
const getOperationStatus = (line, outNo = null) => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: resolveOperationStatusUrl(outNo),
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        operationStatuses = {
            ono: data.ono,
            message_info: data.message_info ? data.message_info.filter(messageInfo =>
                messageInfo.trainline.some(trainline => trainline.name === line)) : [],
            events: data.events ? data.events.filter(event =>
                event.imp_line.some(impLine => impLine.name === line)) : [],
            trans_info: data.trans_info || []
        };
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getOperationStatus';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

=== function getAllLinesNoticeInfo ===
const getAllLinesNoticeInfo = (noticeDeliveryId = null) => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: resolveNoticeInfoUrl(noticeDeliveryId),
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        const isHistoryMode = typeof isHistory !== 'undefined' && isHistory;
        const showInactive = isHistoryMode;
        const showExpired = isHistoryMode;
        allNoticeInfo = filterNoticeList(data.notice_info, showInactive, showExpired);
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getNoticeInfo';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}


=== function getNoticeInfo ===
const getNoticeInfo = (line, noticeDeliveryId = null) => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: resolveNoticeInfoUrl(noticeDeliveryId),
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        const isHistoryMode = typeof isHistory !== 'undefined' && isHistory;
        const showInactive = isHistoryMode;
        const showExpired = isHistoryMode;
        data.notice_info = filterNoticeList(data.notice_info, showInactive, showExpired);
        const noticeInfo = data.notice_info.find(noticeInfo =>
            noticeInfo.trainline.some(
                trainline => trainline.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en') && trainline.name === line)
        );

        noticeInfoLines = noticeInfo ? noticeInfo.notice_infoline.map(noticeInfoline =>
            noticeInfoline.notice_message.find(
                noticeMessage => noticeMessage.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en'))) : [];
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getNoticeInfo';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

const resolveNoticeInfoUrl = (noticeDeliveryId = null) => {
    if (!noticeDeliveryId) {
        return `${NOTICE_PATH}/json/oshirase.json`;
    }

    return `${NOTICE_HISTORY_PATH}/${noticeDeliveryId}/oshirase.json
 - ;
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

const resolveOperationStatusUrl = (outNo = null) => {
    if (!outNo) {
        return `${OPERATION_STATUS_PATH}/json/unkou.json`;
    }

    return `${OPERATION_HISTORY_PATH}/${outNo}/unkou.json`;
}

const resolveTrainPositionsUrl = (date = null, time = null) => {
    if (!date || !time) {
        return `${TRAIN_POSITION_PATH}/zaisenichi.json`;
    }

    return `${TRAIN_POSITION_HISTORY_PATH}/${date}/${time}.json`;
}

const getNoticeInfo = (line, noticeDeliveryId = null) => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: resolveNoticeInfoUrl(noticeDeliveryId),
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        const isHistoryMode = typeof isHistory !== 'undefined' && isHistory;
        const showInactive = isHistoryMode;
        const showExpired = isHistoryMode;
        data.notice_info = filterNoticeList(data.notice_info, showInactive, showExpired);
        const noticeInfo = data.notice_info.find(noticeInfo =>
            noticeInfo.trainline.some(
                trainline => trainline.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en') && trainline.name === line)
        );

        noticeInfoLines = noticeInfo ? noticeInfo.notice_infoline.map(noticeInfoline =>
            noticeInfoline.notice_message.find(
                noticeMessage => noticeMessage.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en'))) : [];
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getNoticeInfo';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

const resolveNoticeInfoUrl = (noticeDeliveryId = null) => {
    if (!noticeDeliveryId) {
        return `${NOTICE_PATH}/json/oshirase.json`;
    }

    return `${NOTICE_HISTORY_PATH}/${noticeDeliveryId}/oshirase.json`;
}

                trainline => trainline.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en') && trainline.name === line)
        );

        noticeInfoLines = noticeInfo ? noticeInfo.notice_infoline.map(noticeInfoline =>
            noticeInfoline.notice_message.find(
                noticeMessage => noticeMessage.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en'))) : [];
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getNoticeInfo';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

const resolveNoticeInfoUrl = (noticeDeliveryId = null) => {
    if (!noticeDeliveryId) {
        return `${NOTICE_PATH}/json/oshirase.json`;
    }

    return `${NOTICE_HISTORY_PATH}/${noticeDeliveryId}/oshirase.json`;
}

        const showExpired = isHistoryMode;
        allNoticeInfo = filterNoticeList(data.notice_info, showInactive, showExpired);
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getNoticeInfo';
    });

const getOperationStatus = (line, outNo = null) => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: resolveOperationStatusUrl(outNo),
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        operationStatuses = {
            ono: data.ono,
            message_info: data.message_info ? data.message_info.filter(messageInfo =>
                messageInfo.trainline.some(trainline => trainline.name === line)) : [],
            events: data.events ? data.events.filter(event =>
                event.imp_line.some(impLine => impLine.name === line)) : [],
            trans_info: data.trans_info || []
        };
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getOperationStatus';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

const getOperationStatus = (line, outNo = null) => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: resolveOperationStatusUrl(outNo),
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        operationStatuses = {
            ono: data.ono,
            message_info: data.message_info ? data.message_info.filter(messageInfo =>
                messageInfo.trainline.some(trainline => trainline.name === line)) : [],
            events: data.events ? data.events.filter(event =>
                event.imp_line.some(impLine => impLine.name === line)) : [],
            trans_info: data.trans_info || []
        };
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getOperationStatus';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

    if (!outNo) {
        return `${OPERATION_STATUS_PATH}/json/unkou.json`;
    }

    return `${OPERATION_HISTORY_PATH}/${outNo}/unkou.json`;
}

    }).done((data) => {
        const isHistoryMode = typeof isHistory !== 'undefined' && isHistory;
        const showInactive = isHistoryMode;
        const showExpired = isHistoryMode;
        data.notice_info = filterNoticeList(data.notice_info, showInactive, showExpired);
        const noticeInfo = data.notice_info.find(noticeInfo =>
            noticeInfo.trainline.some(
                trainline => trainline.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en') && trainline.name === line)
        );

        noticeInfoLines = noticeInfo ? noticeInfo.notice_infoline.map(noticeInfoline =>
            noticeInfoline.notice_message.find(
                noticeMessage => noticeMessage.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en'))) : [];
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getNoticeInfo';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

const getNoticeInfo = (line, noticeDeliveryId = null) => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: resolveNoticeInfoUrl(noticeDeliveryId),
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        const isHistoryMode = typeof isHistory !== 'undefined' && isHistory;
        const showInactive = isHistoryMode;
        const showExpired = isHistoryMode;
        data.notice_info = filterNoticeList(data.notice_info, showInactive, showExpired);
        const noticeInfo = data.notice_info.find(noticeInfo =>
            noticeInfo.trainline.some(

const getNoticeInfo = (line, noticeDeliveryId = null) => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: resolveNoticeInfoUrl(noticeDeliveryId),
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        const isHistoryMode = typeof isHistory !== 'undefined' && isHistory;
        const showInactive = isHistoryMode;
        const showExpired = isHistoryMode;
        data.notice_info = filterNoticeList(data.notice_info, showInactive, showExpired);
        const noticeInfo = data.notice_info.find(noticeInfo =>
            noticeInfo.trainline.some(
                trainline => trainline.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en') && trainline.name === line)
        );

        noticeInfoLines = noticeInfo ? noticeInfo.notice_infoline.map(noticeInfoline =>
            noticeInfoline.notice_message.find(
                noticeMessage => noticeMessage.lang === (paramLang === 'ja' ? paramLang : 'en'))) : [];
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getNoticeInfo';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

        return `${NOTICE_PATH}/json/oshirase.json`;
    }

    return `${NOTICE_HISTORY_PATH}/${noticeDeliveryId}/oshirase.json`;
}

const convertDate = (noSlashDateString) => {
    noSlashDateString = String(noSlashDateString).trim();

    const isValidInput = noSlashDateString.match(/^\d{8}$/) !== null;
    if (!isValidInput) {
        return null;
    }

    const inputYear = parseInt(noSlashDateString.substring(0, 4), 10);
    const inputMonth = parseInt(noSlashDateString.substring(4, 6), 10);
    const inputDay = parseInt(noSlashDateString.substring(6, 8), 10);

    const convertedDate = new Date(inputYear, inputMonth - 1, inputDay);
    convertedDate.setFullYear(inputYear);
    convertedDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

    const isVaildDate = (
        (convertedDate.getFullYear() === inputYear)
        && ((convertedDate.getMonth() + 1) === inputMonth)
        && (convertedDate.getDate() === inputDay)
    );

    if (!isVaildDate) {
        return null;
    }

    return convertedDate;
}

const convertDate = (noSlashDateString) => {
    noSlashDateString = String(noSlashDateString).trim();

    const isValidInput = noSlashDateString.match(/^\d{8}$/) !== null;
    if (!isValidInput) {
        return null;
    }

    const inputYear = parseInt(noSlashDateString.substring(0, 4), 10);
    const inputMonth = parseInt(noSlashDateString.substring(4, 6), 10);
    const inputDay = parseInt(noSlashDateString.substring(6, 8), 10);

    const convertedDate = new Date(inputYear, inputMonth - 1, inputDay);
    convertedDate.setFullYear(inputYear);
    convertedDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

    const isVaildDate = (
        (convertedDate.getFullYear() === inputYear)
        && ((convertedDate.getMonth() + 1) === inputMonth)
        && (convertedDate.getDate() === inputDay)
    );

    if (!isVaildDate) {
        return null;

const checkNoticeDisplayRange = (publicationFrom, publicationTo, showInactive, showExpired) => {
    const today = new Date();
    today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

    const dateFrom = convertDate(publicationFrom);
    const dateTo = convertDate(publicationTo);

    const validFrom = showInactive || ((dateFrom !== null) && (dateFrom <= today));
    const validTo = showExpired || ((dateTo !== null) && (today <= dateTo));
    const isRange = validFrom && validTo;
    return isRange;
}

const filterNoticeList = (noticeList, showInactive, showExpired) => {
    if (showInactive && showExpired) {
        return noticeList;
    }

    noticeList.forEach(train => {
        const filterd = train.notice_infoline.filter((notice) => {
            return checkNoticeDisplayRange(notice.publication_from, notice.publication_to, showInactive, showExpired);
        });
        train.notice_infoline = filterd;
    });

    return noticeList;
}

const getOperationStatus = (line, outNo = null) => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: resolveOperationStatusUrl(outNo),
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        operationStatuses = {
            ono: data.ono,
            message_info: data.message_info ? data.message_info.filter(messageInfo =>
                messageInfo.trainline.some(trainline => trainline.name === line)) : [],
            events: data.events ? data.events.filter(event =>
                event.imp_line.some(impLine => impLine.name === line)) : [],
            trans_info: data.trans_info || []
        };
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'getOperationStatus';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

const resolveOperationStatusUrl = (outNo = null) => {
    if (!outNo) {
        return `${OPERATION_STATUS_PATH}/json/unkou.json`;
    }

    return `${OPERATION_HISTORY_PATH}/${outNo}/unkou.json`;
}

--- around url ---
initLang = (lang = null) => {
    const searchParams = new URLSearchParams(location.search);

    if (lang) {
        paramLang = lang
    } else if (searchParams.get('lang')) {
        paramLang = searchParams.get('lang');
    } else {
        paramLang = 'ja';
    }

    if (!Object.keys(languages).includes(paramLang)) {
        throw 'initLangError';
    }

    return initResources();
}

const initResources = () => {
    const defer = $.Deferred();

    $.ajax({
        url: `${LOCALES_PATH}/${paramLang}/hp_koteimoji_master.json`,
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        success: defer.resolve,
        retries: RETRY_COUNT
    }).done((data) => {
        i18next.init({
            lng: paramLang,
            resources: { [paramLang]: { translation: data } }
        });
    }).fail(() => {
        throw 'initResourcesError';
    });

    return defer.promise();
}

$.ajax = (($orgAjax) => {
    return settings => $orgAjax(settings).fail(function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
        if (textStatus !== 'success') {
            if (--this.retries > 0) {
                setTimeout(() => { $.ajax(this) }, RETRY_INTERVAL);
                return;
            }

            createError();
        }
    })
})($.ajax);

const getText = (key, args = {}) => {
    return i18next.t(key, args);

        await getRequestParameter();

        $.when(
            initLang(),
            getServiceStatus(),
            getHistoryRequestParameter(),
            getLineMasters(),
            getOperationStatus(paramLine, paramOutNo),
            getTransPatterns(),
            getAllLinesNoticeInfo(paramNoticeDeliveryId),
            getNoticeInfo(paramLine, paramNoticeDeliveryId)
        ).then(() => {
            if (!isHistory) {
                createHeader();
                createFooter();
            }
            initMainContents();
        }).fail(() => {
            createError(isHistory ? () => window.open('about:blank', '_self').close() : null);
        });
    } catch (e) {
        createError(isHistory ? () => window.open('about:blank', '_self').close() : null);
    }
});

const initMainContents = () => {
    try {
        if (!existsLineByName(paramLine) && paramRirekiType !== RIREKI_TYPE_OSHIRASE) {
            throw 'invalidLineError';
        }

        $('#foot-error').css('display', 'none');

        if (isOutOfService()) {
            createMaintenance($('.div-status'));
            return;
        }

        if (isHistory) {
            $('main').addClass('history');
        }

        createTrainInformation();
        createNoticeList();
    } catch (e) {
        throw e;
    }
}

const resolveImageFilePath = (image, outNo) => {
    return `${OPERATION_HISTORY_PATH}/${outNo}/${getFileName(image, true)}/${getFileName(image)}`;

const resolveNoticeImageFilePath = (image, lineid, no, lang, timestamp) => {
    if (isHistory) {
        return `${NOTICE_HISTORY_PATH}/${paramNoticeDeliveryId}/${lineid}/${no}/${lang}/${getFileName(image)}?t=${timestamp}`;
    }
    return `${NOTICE_PATH}/${lineid}/${no}/${lang}/${getFileName(image)}?t=${timestamp}`;
}

const createNoticeList = () => {
    if (isHistory && paramRirekiType !== RIREKI_TYPE_OSHIRASE) {
        return;
    }

    if (noticeInfoLines.length > 0) {
        const workNoticeInfoLines = allNoticeInfo.find(

            return;

        let noticeTitleFlag = false
        const timestamp = new Date().getTime();

            const lang = paramLang === 'ja' ? 'ja' : 'en';

            if (noticeMessage && noticeMessage.title) {

                if (!noticeTitleFlag) {
                    noticeTitleFlag = true
                    $('.div-status').append($('<div class="notice-title">')
                        .html(getText('train_information.notice_title')));
                }

                const noticeImage = noticeMessage.image ?
                    $('<div class="notice-image-wrapper">').append($('<img>')
                        .attr('src', resolveNoticeImageFilePath(noticeMessage.image, lineId, workNoticeInfoLines[i].no, lang, timestamp))
                        .on('click', (e) => {

                        })) : null;

                $('.div-status').append($('<div class="notice-list">').append($('<details>')

                            .text(noticeMessage.title)))
                    .append(`<p>${noticeMessage.message.replace(/\n/g, '<br>')}</p>`)
                    .append(noticeImage)));

const getTransInfo = (transInfo, eventNo) => {
    if (!transInfo || !Array.isArray(transInfo)) {
        return null;
    }

    if (eventNo) {
        return transInfo.find(trans => trans.trans_from_line.some(
            line => line.name === paramLine && line.lang === paramLang) && trans.eid === eventNo);
    }
    return transInfo.find(trans => trans.trans_from_line.some(
        line => line.name === paramLine && line.lang === paramLang));
}

const setTransInfo = (transInfo) => {
    if (!transInfo || transInfo.length === 0) {
        return '';
    }

    const html =
        $('<div class="detail-info-container">').append(`
            <span class="detail-info-title">
                ${getText('train_information.transfer_title')}
            </span>
        `);

    return setTransImages(transInfo, html);
}

const setTransImages = (transInfo, html) => {
    const transPtnId = transInfo.trans_ptn_id;

    if (!transPtnId) {
        return;
    }

    const transPattern = transPatterns[transPtnId];

    if (!transPattern) {
        return;
    }

    if (transPattern.disp_img1) {
        html.append(setTransImage(transPattern.disp_img1));
    }

    if (transPattern.disp_img2) {
        html.append(setTransImage(transPattern.disp_img2));
    }

    if (transPattern.disp_img3) {
        html.append(setTransImage(transPattern.disp_img3));
    }

    return html;
}

        return null;
    }

    if (eventNo) {
        return transInfo.find(trans => trans.trans_from_line.some(
            line => line.name === paramLine && line.lang === paramLang) && trans.eid === eventNo);
    }
    return transInfo.find(trans => trans.trans_from_line.some(
        line => line.name === paramLine && line.lang === paramLang));
}

const setTransInfo = (transInfo) => {
    if (!transInfo || transInfo.length === 0) {
        return '';
    }

    const html =
        $('<div class="detail-info-container">').append(`
            <span class="detail-info-title">
                ${getText('train_information.transfer_title')}
            </span>
        `);

    return setTransImages(transInfo, html);
}

const setTransImages = (transInfo, html) => {
    const transPtnId = transInfo.trans_ptn_id;

    if (!transPtnId) {
        return;
    }

    const transPattern = transPatterns[transPtnId];

    if (!transPattern) {
        return;
    }

    if (transPattern.disp_img1) {
        html.append(setTransImage(transPattern.disp_img1));
    }

    if (transPattern.disp_img2) {
        html.append(setTransImage(transPattern.disp_img2));
    }

    if (transPattern.disp_img3) {
        html.append(setTransImage(transPattern.disp_img3));
    }

    return html;
}

const getRequestParameter = async () => {
    const searchParams = new URLSearchParams(location.search);

    lineId = conversionLineParam.externalToInternal[searchParams.get('line')];
    paramLang = searchParams.get('lang') ? searchParams.get('lang') : 'ja';
    if (lineId && lineId !== ISE_RAILWAY_LINE_ID) {
        const lineMaster = await resolveLineMasterByLang(lineId, paramLang);
        if (lineId === TOKAIDO_ATAMI_TOYOHASHI_LINE_ID ||
            lineId === TOKAIDO_TOYOHASHI_MAIBARA_LINE_ID) {
            paramLine = `${lineMaster?.ryokakuSenkuMei + LINE_NAME_KUKAN_START + lineMaster?.ryokakuSenkuKaishiShuryoEki + LINE_NAME_KUKAN_END}`;
        } else if (lineId === ZENSEN_LINE_ID) {
            paramLine = paramLang === 'ja' ? ZENSEN_LINE_NAME_JA : ZENSEN_LINE_NAME_EN;
        } else {
            paramLine = lineMaster?.ryokakuSenkuMei
        }
    } else {
        throw 'paramError';
    }
}

const getHistoryRequestParameter = () => {
    const searchParams = new URLSearchParams(location.search);

    if (searchParams.has('rireki_type')) {
        paramRirekiType = searchParams.get('rireki_type');

        if (paramRirekiType !== RIREKI_TYPE_UNKOU && paramRirekiType !== RIREKI_TYPE_OSHIRASE) {
            throw 'historyParamError';
        }

        if (paramLang !== 'ja' && paramLang !== 'en') {
            throw 'historyParamError';
        }

        if (paramRirekiType === RIREKI_TYPE_UNKOU) {
            paramOutNo = searc
